The hotel is beautiful & clean, the bed is comfortable and it has a  kitchen, a washing machine, it is specious & has a lot of natural light coming in through the wide window I had in my chosen room. 

I booked two nights for a staycation and the price was about ¬•1300 including breakfast. Breakfast was a mixture of both western & Chinese style. I really cannot complain about the food range. 

The hotel is easy to find as the taxi drops you close by and there are shops downstairs(restaurants, coffee shops & a supermarket) 
On my 2nd night I decided to cook, which was great. 

One of the nights I had a delivery and the gentleman down stairs sent it with a robot. 

The service overall is great. The staff can speak a decent amount of English which made it easy for me as a non Chinese speaker. Because of how central the hotel is I even went to get my nails done, which was at a walking distance. However because of the highway next to the hotel , you can hear the cars so it can be noisy sometimes. 

The hotel has a gym ,an indoor pool ,lounge area ( amongst other things) 

I would recommend this hotel for solo travels, couples and friends. 
I‚Äôm giving it 4/5 overall because they will need to have an outdoor pool to get a 5.

Just like a "home" settled in Suzhou

During the morning rush hour, there may not be enough tables when there are many people, and meals may not be served in time. Fortunately, there are many famous Suzhou snacks and noodle restaurants around. If you think about it this way, you don't have to eat too much for breakfast.

Parking in the hotel is also very convenient. The ground parking lot downstairs is preferred. If it is full, you can park in the underground parking lot.

Downstairs is Vanke Plaza, which is very convenient for shopping and eating.
